         <h1 id="omnibus-gitlab-docs">Omnibus GitLab Docs<a href="#omnibus-gitlab-docs" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h1> 
         <p>Omnibus GitLab is a way to package different services and tools required to run GitLab, so that most users can install it without laborious configuration. </p>
         <h2 id="package-information">Package information<a href="#package-information" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="package-information/README.html#checking-the-versions-of-bundled-software">Checking the versions of bundled software</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/defaults.html">Package defaults</a> </li>
          <li><a href="/13.12/ee/development/architecture.html#component-list">Components included</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/deprecated_os.html">Deprecated Operating Systems</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/signed_packages.html">Signed Packages</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/deprecation_policy.html">Deprecation Policy</a> </li>
          <li><a href="https://gitlab-org.gitlab.io/omnibus-gitlab/licenses.html">Licenses of bundled dependencies</a> </li>
         </ul> 
         <h2 id="installation">Installation<a href="#installation" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>For installation details, see <a href="installation/index.html">Installing Omnibus GitLab</a>. </p>
         <h2 id="running-on-a-low-resource-device-like-a-raspberry-pi">Running on a low-resource device (like a Raspberry Pi)<a href="#running-on-a-low-resource-device-like-a-raspberry-pi" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>You can run GitLab on supported low-resource computers like the Raspberry Pi 3, but you must tune the settings to work best with the available resources. Check out the <a href="settings/rpi.html">documentation</a> for suggestions on what to adjust. </p>
         <h2 id="maintenance">Maintenance<a href="#maintenance" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#get-service-status">Get service status</a> </li>

          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#invoking-rake-tasks">Invoking Rake tasks</a> </li>
          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#starting-a-rails-console-session">Starting a Rails console session</a> </li>
          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#starting-a-postgresql-superuser-psql-session">Starting a PostgreSQL superuser <code class="highlighter-rouge">psql</code> session</a> </li>
          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#container-registry-garbage-collection">Container registry garbage collection</a> </li>
         </ul>

         <h2 id="troubleshooting">Troubleshooting<a href="#troubleshooting" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2>

          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#apt-error-the-requested-url-returned-error-403">Apt error: <code class="highlighter-rouge">The requested URL returned error: 403</code></a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#gitlab-is-unreachable-in-my-browser">GitLab is unreachable in my browser</a>. </li>

          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#reconfigure-freezes-at-ruby_blocksupervise_redis_sleep-action-run">Reconfigure freezes at ruby_block[supervise_redis_sleep] action run</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#tcp-ports-for-gitlab-services-are-already-taken">TCP ports for GitLab services are already taken</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#selinux-enabled-systems">Git SSH access stops working on SELinux-enabled systems</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#postgresql-error-fatal--could-not-create-shared-memory-segment-cannot-allocate-memory">PostgreSQL error <code class="highlighter-rouge">FATAL: could not create shared memory segment: Cannot allocate memory</code></a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#reconfigure-complains-about-the-glibc-version">Reconfigure complains about the GLIBC version</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#reconfigure-fails-to-create-the-git-user">Reconfigure fails to create the Git user</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#failed-to-modify-kernel-parameters-with-sysctl">Failed to modify kernel parameters with sysctl</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#i-am-unable-to-install-omnibus-gitlab-without-root-access">I am unable to install Omnibus GitLab without root access</a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#gitlab-rake-assetsprecompile-fails-with-permission-denied"><code class="highlighter-rouge">gitlab-rake assets:precompile</code> fails with <code class="highlighter-rouge">Permission denied</code></a>. </li>
          <li> <a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#short-read-or-oom-loading-db-error"><code class="highlighter-rouge">Short read or OOM loading DB</code> error</a>. </li>
          <li><a href="settings/database.html#using-a-non-packaged-postgresql-database-management-server"><code class="highlighter-rouge">pg_dump: aborting because of server version mismatch</code></a> </li>
          <li><a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#errnoenomem-cannot-allocate-memory-during-backup-or-upgrade"><code class="highlighter-rouge">Errno::ENOMEM: Cannot allocate memory</code> during backup or upgrade</a> </li>
          <li><a href="common_installation_problems/README.html#nginx-error-could-not-build-server_names_hash-you-should-increase-s
